attempt < callOpts.max; attempt++ {\n55: \t\t\tif err := waitRetryBackoff(ctx, attempt, callOpts); err != nil {\n56: \t\t\t\treturn err\n57: \t\t\t}\n58: \t\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\n59: \t\t\t\t\"retrying of unary invoker\",\n60: \t\t\t\tzap.String(\"target\", cc.Target()),\n61: \t\t\t\tzap.String(\"method\", method),\n62: \t\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt),\n63: \t\t\t)\n64: \t\t\tlastErr = invoker(ctx, method, req, reply, cc, grpcOpts...)\n65: \t\t\tif lastErr == nil {\n66: \t\t\t\treturn nil\n67: \t\t\t}\n68: \t\t\tc.GetLogger().Warn(\n69: \t\t\t\t\"retrying of unary invoker failed\",\n70: \t\t\t\tzap.String(\"target\", cc.Target()),\n71: \t\t\t\tzap.String(\"peer\", p.String()),\n72: \t\t\t\tzap.String(\"method\", method),\n73: \t\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt),\n74: \t\t\t\tzap.Error(lastErr),\n75: \t\t\t)\n76: \t\t\tif isContextError(lastErr) {\n77: \t\t\t\tif ctx.Err() != nil {\n78: \t\t\t\t\t// its the context deadline or cancellation.\n79: \t\t\t\t\treturn lastErr\n80: \t\t\t\t}\n81: \t\t\t\t// its the callCtx deadline or cancellation, in which case try again.\n82: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n83: \t\t\t}\n84: \t\t\tif c.shouldRefreshToken(lastErr, callOpts) {\n85: \t\t\t\tgtErr := c.refreshToken(ctx)\n86: \t\t\t\tif gtErr != nil {\n87: \t\t\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Warn(\n88: \t\t\t\t\t\t\"retrying of unary invoker failed to fetch new auth token\",\n89: \t\t\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"target\", cc.Target()),\n90: \t\t\t\t\t\tzap.Error(gtErr),\n91: \t\t\t\t\t)\n92: \t\t\t\t\treturn gtErr // lastErr must be invalid auth token\n93: \t\t\t\t}\n94: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n95: \t\t\t}\n96: \t\t\tif !isSafeRetry(c, lastErr, callOpts) {\n97: \t\t\t\treturn lastErr\n98: \t\t\t}\n99: \t\t}\n100: \t\treturn lastErr\n101: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/etcd-io/etcd@a5ca6f1bbe98d06c33d7b21b0522decaa265e25c/-/blob/client/v3/retry_interceptor.go%3FL1-100"}}}

\"text\": \"# etcd Client-Side Retry and Timeout Policy Implementation\\n\\nThe etcd-io/etcd repository implements comprehensive client-side retry and timeout policies through multiple interconnected components:\\n\\n## gRPC Retry Interceptors\\n\\n**client/v3/retry_interceptor.go** contains the core retry logic:\\n- `unaryClientInterceptor()`: Handles retry for unary RPC calls (Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations) with configurable max retries and exponential backoff\\n- `streamClientInterceptor()`: Handles retry for streaming RPC calls (Watch operations) with disabled retries by default for safety\\n- `waitRetryBackoff()`: Implements backoff logic between retry attempts with jitter to prevent thundering herd\\n\\n## Retry Policy and Error Handling\\n\\n**client/v3/retry.go** defines the retry semantics:\\n- `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()`: Determines if immutable requests (Read operations) can be safely retried. Returns true only for Unavailable errors, otherwise stops retry to prevent duplicate reads\\n- `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()`: Determines if mutable requests (Write operations) can be safely retried. Only retries on Unavailable when initial connection failed, never on established connections to preserve write-at-most-once semantics\\n- `retryKVClient`: Wraps KV client with retry logic for Put, Range, Delete, Txn operations\\n- `retryWatchClient`: Wraps Watch client with retry logic for Watch streams\\n- `retryLeaseClient`: Wraps Lease client with retry logic for Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations\\n\\n## Endpoint Balancer and Health Check\\n\\n**client/v3/client.go** implements the endpoint management and health checking:\\n- `dialWithBalancer()`: Dials the client's current load-balanced resolver group using gRPC's built-in round-robin balancer\\n- `autoSync()`: Periodic endpoint synchronization (when AutoSyncInterval > 0) that fetches fresh cluster member information from the server\\n- `waitForConnection()`: Waits for gRPC connection to be ready using the health check service, with fallback for servers not exposing health endpoints\\n- `dialSetupOpts()`: Configures gRPC dial options including:\\n  - keepalive parameters (Time, Timeout, PermitWithoutStream)\\n  - transport credentials (TLS)\\n  - unary/stream interceptors with retry and backoff settings\\n\\n## Configuration and Timeout Settings\\n\\n**client/v3/config.go** defines timeout and retry configuration:\\n- `DialTimeout`: Timeout for initial connection establishment\\n- `DialKeepAliveTime`: Interval for client-side keepalive pings to detect broken connections\\n- `DialKeepAliveTimeout`: Timeout waiting for keepalive response before closing connection\\n- `MaxUnaryRetries`: Maximum retry attempts for unary calls (default: 3)\\n- `BackoffWaitBetween`: Base wait duration between retries\\n- `BackoffJitterFraction`: Jitter fraction to randomize backoff timing\\n\\n## KV, Watch, and Lease Operation Implementations\\n\\n**client/v3/kv.go**: Defines KV interface with Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations that use the wrapped retryKVClient\\n\\n**client/v3/watch.go**: Implements Watch interface for server push notifications, handles stream resumption on connection failures with closeSendErrTimeout (250ms)\\n\\n**client/v3/lease.go**: Implements Lease interface with Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations and keepAliveTimeout parameter for KeepAlive stream management. The `sendKeepAliveLoop()` sends periodic keep-alive requests to maintain lease liveliness.\\n\\n## Endpoint Resolution and Management\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go**: Implements EtcdManualResolver using gRPC's manual.Builder for endpoint state management and updates\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/resolver/resolver.go**: Provides gRPC resolver builder using etcd's endpoint manager for dynamic endpoint discovery\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go**: Interprets endpoint URLs (http, https, unix, unixs) and manages credentials requirements (CredsRequire, CredsDrop, CredsOptional)\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/endpoints/endpoints.go**: Manager interface for dynamically adding/deleting/listing endpoints backed by etcd storage\\n\\n## Overall Request Flow\\n\\n1. Client initialization calls `dialWithBalancer()` which uses the resolver to discover endpoints\\n2. `waitForConnection()` ensures the connection is healthy via gRPC health checks\\n3. `autoSync()` periodically refreshes endpoints in background\\n4. Unary calls go through `unaryClientInterceptor()` which applies retry logic with backoff\\n5. Stream calls (Watch) go through `streamClientInterceptor()` with retries disabled by default\\n6. `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()` and `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()` guard retry decisions based on error type\\n7. KV operations use `retryKVClient`, Watch uses `retryWatchClient`, Lease uses `retryLeaseClient`\\n8. gRPC keepalive parameters ensure timely detection of broken connections\\n9. Lease keep-alive loop maintains lease TTL with `sendKeepAliveLoop()`\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2063,"cache_read_input_tokens":97017,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2063},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"22b101e7-9750-4e4d-87db-bb87dc4eedaa","uuid":"78b53a5d-6949-43d6-bc1a-1b32a178254d"}

semantics:\\n- `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()`: Determines if immutable requests (Read operations) can be safely retried. Returns true only for Unavailable errors, otherwise stops retry to prevent duplicate reads\\n- `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()`: Determines if mutable requests (Write operations) can be safely retried. Only retries on Unavailable when initial connection failed, never on established connections to preserve write-at-most-once semantics\\n- `retryKVClient`: Wraps KV client with retry logic for Put, Range, Delete, Txn operations\\n- `retryWatchClient`: Wraps Watch client with retry logic for Watch streams\\n- `retryLeaseClient`: Wraps Lease client with retry logic for Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations\\n\\n## Endpoint Balancer and Health Check\\n\\n**client/v3/client.go** implements the endpoint management and health checking:\\n- `dialWithBalancer()`: Dials the client's current load-balanced resolver group using gRPC's built-in round-robin balancer\\n- `autoSync()`: Periodic endpoint synchronization (when AutoSyncInterval > 0) that fetches fresh cluster member information from the server\\n- `waitForConnection()`: Waits for gRPC connection to be ready using the health check service, with fallback for servers not exposing health endpoints\\n- `dialSetupOpts()`: Configures gRPC dial options including:\\n  - keepalive parameters (Time, Timeout, PermitWithoutStream)\\n  - transport credentials (TLS)\\n  - unary/stream interceptors with retry and backoff settings\\n\\n## Configuration and Timeout Settings\\n\\n**client/v3/config.go** defines timeout and retry configuration:\\n- `DialTimeout`: Timeout for initial connection establishment\\n- `DialKeepAliveTime`: Interval for client-side keepalive pings to detect broken connections\\n- `DialKeepAliveTimeout`: Timeout waiting for keepalive response before closing connection\\n- `MaxUnaryRetries`: Maximum retry attempts for unary calls (default: 3)\\n- `BackoffWaitBetween`: Base wait duration between retries\\n- `BackoffJitterFraction`: Jitter fraction to randomize backoff timing\\n\\n## KV, Watch, and Lease Operation Implementations\\n\\n**client/v3/kv.go**: Defines KV interface with Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations that use the wrapped retryKVClient\\n\\n**client/v3/watch.go**: Implements Watch interface for server push notifications, handles stream resumption on connection failures with closeSendErrTimeout (250ms)\\n\\n**client/v3/lease.go**: Implements Lease interface with Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations and keepAliveTimeout parameter for KeepAlive stream management. The `sendKeepAliveLoop()` sends periodic keep-alive requests to maintain lease liveliness.\\n\\n## Endpoint Resolution and Management\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go**: Implements EtcdManualResolver using gRPC's manual.Builder for endpoint state management and updates\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/resolver/resolver.go**: Provides gRPC resolver builder using etcd's endpoint manager for dynamic endpoint discovery\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go**: Interprets endpoint URLs (http, https, unix, unixs) and manages credentials requirements (CredsRequire, CredsDrop, CredsOptional)\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/endpoints/endpoints.go**: Manager interface for dynamically adding/deleting/listing endpoints backed by etcd storage\\n\\n## Overall Request Flow\\n\\n1. Only retries on Unavailable when initial connection failed, never on established connections to preserve write-at-most-once semantics\\n- `retryKVClient`: Wraps KV client with retry logic for Put, Range, Delete, Txn operations\\n- `retryWatchClient`: Wraps Watch client with retry logic for Watch streams\\n- `retryLeaseClient`: Wraps Lease client with retry logic for Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations\\n\\n## Endpoint Balancer and Health Check\\n\\n**client/v3/client.go** implements the endpoint management and health checking:\\n- `dialWithBalancer()`: Dials the client's current load-balanced resolver group using gRPC's built-in round-robin balancer\\n- `autoSync()`: Periodic endpoint synchronization (when AutoSyncInterval > 0) that fetches fresh cluster member information from the server\\n- `waitForConnection()`: Waits for gRPC connection to be ready using the health check service, with fallback for servers not exposing health endpoints\\n- `dialSetupOpts()`: Configures gRPC dial options including:\\n  - keepalive parameters (Time, Timeout, PermitWithoutStream)\\n  - transport credentials (TLS)\\n  - unary/stream interceptors with retry and backoff settings\\n\\n## Configuration and Timeout Settings\\n\\n**client/v3/config.go** defines timeout and retry configuration:\\n- `DialTimeout`: Timeout for initial connection establishment\\n- `DialKeepAliveTime`: Interval for client-side keepalive pings to detect broken connections\\n- `DialKeepAliveTimeout`: Timeout waiting for keepalive response before closing connection\\n- `MaxUnaryRetries`: Maximum retry attempts for unary calls (default: 3)\\n- `BackoffWaitBetween`: Base wait duration between retries\\n- `BackoffJitterFraction`: Jitter fraction to randomize backoff timing\\n\\n## KV, Watch, and Lease Operation Implementations\\n\\n**client/v3/kv.go**: Defines KV interface with Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations that use the wrapped retryKVClient\\n\\n**client/v3/watch.go**: Implements Watch interface for server push notifications, handles stream resumption on connection failures with closeSendErrTimeout (250ms)\\n\\n**client/v3/lease.go**: Implements Lease interface with Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations and keepAliveTimeout parameter for KeepAlive stream management. The `sendKeepAliveLoop()` sends periodic keep-alive requests to maintain lease liveliness.\\n\\n## Endpoint Resolution and Management\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go**: Implements EtcdManualResolver using gRPC's manual.Builder for endpoint state management and updates\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/resolver/resolver.go**: Provides gRPC resolver builder using etcd's endpoint manager for dynamic endpoint discovery\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go**: Interprets endpoint URLs (http, https, unix, unixs) and manages credentials requirements (CredsRequire, CredsDrop, CredsOptional)\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/endpoints/endpoints.go**: Manager interface for dynamically adding/deleting/listing endpoints backed by etcd storage\\n\\n## Overall Request Flow\\n\\n1. Client initialization calls `dialWithBalancer()` which uses the resolver to discover endpoints\\n2. `waitForConnection()` ensures the connection is healthy via gRPC health checks\\n3. `autoSync()` periodically refreshes endpoints in background\\n4. Unary calls go through `unaryClientInterceptor()` which applies retry logic with backoff\\n5. Stream calls (Watch) go through `streamClientInterceptor()` with retries disabled by default\\n6. `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()` and `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()` guard retry decisions based on error type\\n7. KV operations use `retryKVClient`, Watch uses `retryWatchClient`, Lease uses `retryLeaseClient`\\n8. gRPC keepalive parameters ensure timely detection of broken connections\\n9. Lease keep-alive loop maintains lease TTL with `sendKeepAliveLoop()`\"\n}\n","numLines":48,"startLine":1,"totalLines":48}}}
